WITH RECURSIVE branch(id, parent_id, turn_id, role, content, depth) AS (
  SELECT id, parent_id, turn_id, role, content, 0
  FROM normandy_session_entries WHERE id = $1
  UNION ALL

  FROM normandy_session_entries e

)
